<p><b>Ciro Immobile</b> (<small>Italian pronunciation:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Italian" title="Help:IPA/Italian">[tiro immbile]</a></span>; born 20 February 1990) is an Italian professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Striker" title="Forward (association football)">striker</a> for <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> club <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy national team</a>.
</p><p>Immobile began his career at <a href="/wiki/Sorrento_Calcio" class="mw-redirect" title="Sorrento Calcio">Sorrento</a>. In 2009, he was purchased by <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>, and was later loaned out to three <a href="/wiki/Serie_B" title="Serie B">Serie B</a> clubs, including <a href="/wiki/Delfino_Pescara_1936" title="Delfino Pescara 1936">Pescara</a>, with whom he won the league title as the top-scorer, before moving to <a href="/wiki/Genoa_C.F.C." title="Genoa C.F.C.">Genoa</a> in 2012. After a season with the club, he moved to Juventus' rivals <a href="/wiki/Torino_F.C." title="Torino F.C.">Torino</a>. At Torino, he won the <i><a href="/wiki/Capocannoniere" title="Capocannoniere">Capocannoniere</a></i> award for the top scorer in Serie A. After his breakout season at Torino, he was sold to German club <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> for around 18 million in 2014, where he won the <a href="/wiki/DFL-Supercup" title="DFL-Supercup">DFL-Supercup</a>, before moving to Spanish club <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a> in 2015. In 2016, he returned to Torino on loan, and was later sold to Lazio in July of that year. In his second season at Lazio, he won the <i>Capocannoniere</i> for a second time, with 29 goals in 33 games. The <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_S.S._Lazio_season" title="201920 S.S. Lazio season">201920 season</a> was the most prolific of Immobile's career; he equalled the record for <a href="/wiki/Football_records_and_statistics_in_Italy#Most_goals_in_a_single_Serie_A_season" title="Football records and statistics in Italy">most Serie A goals in a season</a> with 36, and won a third <i>Capocannoniere</i> title and first <a href="/wiki/European_Golden_Shoe" title="European Golden Shoe">European Golden Shoe</a>, given to the top scorer in Europe. Immobile has also won a <a href="/wiki/Coppa_Italia" title="Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a> and two <a href="/wiki/Supercoppa_Italiana" title="Supercoppa Italiana">Supercoppa Italiana</a> titles with Lazio.
</p><p>Immobile made his debut for the <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italian national team</a> in 2014, and was included in the squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a> and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sorrento_and_Juventus">Sorrento and Juventus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Sorrento and Juventus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Born in <a href="/wiki/Torre_Annunziata" title="Torre Annunziata">Torre Annunziata</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/Province_of_Naples" title="Province of Naples">province of Naples</a>, Immobile began his youth career in the football school "Torre Annunziata '88", before transferring to "Maria Rosa" and finally the youth team of <a href="/wiki/U.S._Salernitana_1919" title="U.S. Salernitana 1919">Salernitana</a>, where however, he failed to emerge.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> He later joined Sorrento,<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> with whom he scored 30 goals in the under-17 during the 200708 season, including a brace against Torino, impressing the observers of Juventus.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2008, he was signed at the age of 18 for 80,000<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> by Juventus under the recommendation of <a href="/wiki/Ciro_Ferrara" title="Ciro Ferrara">Ciro Ferrara</a>. He went on to play with the <a href="/wiki/Campionato_Nazionale_Primavera" title="Campionato Nazionale Primavera"><i>Primavera</i></a> formation.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ciro_Immobile_crop.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Ciro_Immobile_crop.jpg/170px-Ciro_Immobile_crop.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="347" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Ciro_Immobile_crop.jpg/255px-Ciro_Immobile_crop.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Ciro_Immobile_crop.jpg/340px-Ciro_Immobile_crop.jpg 2x" data-file-width="669" data-file-height="1366" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ciro_Immobile_crop.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Immobile with Juventus in August 2011</div></div></div>
<p>Immobile joined the <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C._Youth_Sector" title="Juventus F.C. Youth Sector">Primavera</a> squad in 2009, where he formed a striking partnership with <a href="/wiki/Ayub_Daud" title="Ayub Daud">Ayub Daud</a>, that led the squad to win the <a href="/wiki/Torneo_di_Viareggio_2009" class="mw-redirect" title="Torneo di Viareggio 2009">2009 Torneo di Viareggio</a>, where he scored a total five goals; two of which came in the final.<sup id="cite_ref-tor09_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tor09-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 14 March 2009, Immobile made his <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> debut in a 41 home win against <a href="/wiki/Bologna_F.C._1909" title="Bologna F.C. 1909">Bologna</a>, replacing Juventus' captain <a href="/wiki/Alessandro_Del_Piero" title="Alessandro Del Piero">Alessandro Del Piero</a> in the 89th minute.
On 25 November 2009, Immobile also made his debut in a <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">European</a> competition, once again as a second-half substitute for Del Piero in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> game against <a href="/wiki/FC_Girondins_de_Bordeaux" title="FC Girondins de Bordeaux">Bordeaux</a>. In February 2010, he scored a <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> against <a href="/wiki/Empoli_F.C." title="Empoli F.C.">Empoli</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2010_Torneo_di_Viareggio" title="2010 Torneo di Viareggio">2010 Torneo di Viareggio</a> final to seal the title for a second consecutive season.<sup id="cite_ref-tor10_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tor10-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Loans_to_Siena_and_Grosseto">Loans to Siena and Grosseto</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Loans to Siena and Grosseto">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 1 July 2010, Immobile, along with teammate <a href="/wiki/Luca_Marrone" title="Luca Marrone">Luca Marrone</a>, were sent on loan to recently relegated <a href="/wiki/Serie_B" title="Serie B">Serie B</a> side <a href="/wiki/A.C._Siena" class="mw-redirect" title="A.C. Siena">A.C. Siena</a>. In exchange for the two loans, Juventus acquired <a href="/wiki/Niccol%C3%B2_Giannetti" title="Niccolò Giannetti">Niccolò Giannetti</a>, <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_Spinazzola" title="Leonardo Spinazzola">Leonardo Spinazzola</a>, and Austrian midfielder <a href="/wiki/Marcel_B%C3%BCchel" title="Marcel Büchel">Marcel Büchel</a> on loan from the Tuscan club.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Immobile never broke into the first team, however, and in January 2011, he left Siena, after just 4 appearances and 1 goal. Following his departure from Siena, he was immediately loaned by Juventus to <a href="/wiki/U.S._Grosseto_F.C." class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Grosseto F.C.">Grosseto</a>, another Serie B club for the remainder of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Serie_B" title="201011 Serie B">201011 Serie B</a> season.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Loan_to_Pescara">Loan to Pescara</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Loan to Pescara">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 17 August 2011, it was announced that Immobile would join <a href="/wiki/Serie_B" title="Serie B">Serie B</a> club <a href="/wiki/Delfino_Pescara_1936" title="Delfino Pescara 1936">Pescara</a> on a season-long loan from Juventus.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first goal for the club on 26 August during his debut for Pescara in the first league match against <a href="/wiki/Hellas_Verona_F.C." title="Hellas Verona F.C.">Hellas Verona</a>. By the end of the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Serie_B" title="201112 Serie B">201112 Serie B</a> <i>andata</i> (first half of the season), Immobile had already scored 14 league goals. On 30 January 2012, <a href="/wiki/Genoa_C.F.C." title="Genoa C.F.C.">Genoa</a> confirmed that they had paid 4 million for half of the player's rights from Juventus, following his mercurial form in Serie B. He completed his season with Pescara in the Italian second division, as the club won the league title and sealed promotion to <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a>. He also went on to become the Serie B season's top scorer with a total of 28 goals, seven more than the second-highest scorer, <a href="/wiki/S.S._Juve_Stabia" title="S.S. Juve Stabia">Juve Stabia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Marco_Sau" title="Marco Sau">Marco Sau</a>. Immobile was also named Serie B's Player of the Year at the <a href="/wiki/Oscar_del_Calcio" class="mw-redirect" title="Oscar del Calcio">2012 AIC Gran Gala del Calcio</a>, alongside teammates <a href="/wiki/Lorenzo_Insigne" title="Lorenzo Insigne">Lorenzo Insigne</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marco_Verratti" title="Marco Verratti">Marco Verratti</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-poy12_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-poy12-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Genoa">Genoa</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Genoa">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Immobile formally became a Genoa player on 1 July 2012 after the loan with Pescara expired. On 19 June 2013, Genoa and Juventus again renewed the co-ownership agreements of Immobile and Boakye.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Torino">Torino</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Torino">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 12 July 2013 Juventus bought Genoa's half of Immobile for 2.75 million.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> On the same day he was sold to city-rivals <a href="/wiki/Torino_F.C." title="Torino F.C.">Torino</a> under a new co-ownership deal for 2.75 million.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He made his debut for Torino during the first round of the <a href="/wiki/Coppa_Italia" title="Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a> against former club Pescara, scoring his first goal of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He provided an assist in his Serie A debut for the club, but did not score until 7 October in a 22 draw against <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a>. Previously, Immobile had failed to score in Serie A since December 2012. The goal signalled a run of form for Immobile, with the player scoring a further 12 goals in his next 15 matches, including his first brace in Serie A during a game against <a href="/wiki/Chievo_Verona" class="mw-redirect" title="Chievo Verona">Chievo Verona</a> in December.<sup id="cite_ref-sway_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sway-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 22 March 2014, Immobile scored his first Serie A hat-trick, in a 31 win against <a href="/wiki/A.S._Livorno_Calcio" title="A.S. Livorno Calcio">Livorno</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he scored a spectacular volley with his left foot against <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a>, temporarily bringing the <i>Granata</i> level at the <a href="/wiki/Stadio_Olimpico" title="Stadio Olimpico">Stadio Olimpico</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> On 6 April, he scored the winning goal against <a href="/wiki/Calcio_Catania" title="Calcio Catania">Catania</a> in a 21 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 April, Genoa were leading 10, when Immobile and <a href="/wiki/Alessio_Cerci" title="Alessio Cerci">Alessio Cerci</a> both scored in stoppage time to give Torino a 21 win.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> He scored again in the following round in a 33 draw away to <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-lazio_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lazio-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> On 27 April, Immobile scored for the sixth consecutive match in a 20 defeat of <a href="/wiki/Udinese_Calcio" title="Udinese Calcio">Udinese</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> This took him to 21 goals in the season,<sup id="cite_ref-21st_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21st-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> equaling the seasonal goal records of <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Pulici" title="Paolo Pulici">Paolo Pulici</a> and <a href="/wiki/Francesco_Graziani" title="Francesco Graziani">Francesco Graziani</a> at Torino.<sup id="cite_ref-21-record_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21-record-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 May, Immobile scored in the penultimate fixture of the season against <a href="/wiki/Parma_F.C." class="mw-redirect" title="Parma F.C.">Parma</a>, but was sent off in the second half and suspended for the final match against <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He concluded his season with 22 goals in 33 appearances, plus one goal in the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Coppa_Italia" title="201314 Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-soccerway-profile_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soccerway-profile-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> He became the first Torino player to win the <i><a href="/wiki/Capocannoniere" title="Capocannoniere">Capocannoniere</a></i> since <a href="/wiki/Francesco_Graziani" title="Francesco Graziani">Francesco Graziani</a> in the <a href="/wiki/1976%E2%80%9377_Serie_A" title="197677 Serie A">197677 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-tgs14_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tgs14-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Borussia_Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Borussia Dortmund">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ciro-immobile-bvb-2014.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Ciro-immobile-bvb-2014.jpg/220px-Ciro-immobile-bvb-2014.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Ciro-immobile-bvb-2014.jpg/330px-Ciro-immobile-bvb-2014.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Ciro-immobile-bvb-2014.jpg/440px-Ciro-immobile-bvb-2014.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3000" data-file-height="2000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ciro-immobile-bvb-2014.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Immobile playing for Borussia Dortmund in July 2014</div></div></div>
<p>On 2 June 2014 <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> club <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> announced the signing of Immobile,<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-zorc_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-zorc-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> despite the co-ownership agreement between Torino and Juventus not being resolved. <a href="/wiki/Urbano_Cairo" title="Urbano Cairo">Urbano Cairo</a>, the president of Torino, accused Juventus and Dortmund of violating FIFA regulation regarding transfer on 10 May 2014,<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> which <a href="/wiki/FIGC" class="mw-redirect" title="FIGC">FIGC</a> also states that such transfers must have mutual consent of the co-owners. Cairo also wanted to keep Immobile for at least a season for sports and for profit. On 18 June 2014,<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Juventus sold the remaining 50% registration rights of Immobile to Torino for 8.035 million.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Torino later revealed in its financial filing, that the transfer fee to the German side was 17.955 million.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> On 13 August 2014, Immobile made his official debut for Dortmund as a striker in the starting line up for the 2014 DFL-Supercup against Bayern Munich. The match ended in Borussia lifting the cup by the score of 20.<sup id="cite_ref-scup14_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-scup14-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Immobile made his Bundesliga debut on 23 August in the opening match of Dortmund's <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Bundesliga" title="201415 Bundesliga">201415 Bundesliga</a> campaign which saw them lose 20 to <a href="/wiki/Bayer_Leverkusen" class="mw-redirect" title="Bayer Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a> at home. On 16 September 2014, Immobile scored his first goal for the club, opening a 20 home win over <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> in the group stages of the Champions League.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
He scored four goals in six Champions League matches,<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> in a 30 away win over <a href="/wiki/R.S.C._Anderlecht" title="R.S.C. Anderlecht">Anderlecht</a>, in a 41 home win over <a href="/wiki/Galatasaray_S.K._(football)" title="Galatasaray S.K. (football)">Galatasaray</a> and in a 11 home draw vs <a href="/wiki/R.S.C._Anderlecht" title="R.S.C. Anderlecht">Anderlecht</a>, with Borussia qualifying as first from the group. On 17 December 2014, Immobile assisted the first goal and scored the second on a 22 home draw with <a href="/wiki/VfL_Wolfsburg" title="VfL Wolfsburg">Wolfsburg</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sevilla">Sevilla</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Sevilla">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_-_Ciro_Immobile_(2).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_-_Ciro_Immobile_%282%29.jpg/220px-2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_-_Ciro_Immobile_%282%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_-_Ciro_Immobile_%282%29.jpg/330px-2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_-_Ciro_Immobile_%282%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/7/7a/2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_-_Ciro_Immobile_%282%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="370" data-file-height="370" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_-_Ciro_Immobile_(2).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Immobile with Sevilla in August 2015, prior to the UEFA Super Cup</div></div></div>
<p>On 12 July 2015, Immobile joined <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a> on a season-long loan after scoring just three goals in the league in his first season at Borussia Dortmund, with a total 10 goals in 34 matches across all competitions.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Sevilla also had an option to sign him outright. He made his debut for the club on 11 August 2015, coming off the bench to replace <a href="/wiki/Kevin_Gameiro" title="Kevin Gameiro">Kevin Gameiro</a> in the 80th minute of the <a href="/wiki/2015_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2015 UEFA Super Cup">2015 UEFA Super Cup</a> final, against <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, and assisting <a href="/wiki/Yevhen_Konoplyanka" title="Yevhen Konoplyanka">Yevhen Konoplyanka</a>'s temporary equaliser to send the match into extra-time; Barcelona went on to win the match 54.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 31 July 2015, Immobile was stretchered off the pitch wearing an <a href="/wiki/Oxygen_mask" title="Oxygen mask">oxygen mask</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Cervical_collar" title="Cervical collar">neck brace</a> after playing just five minutes in a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a> at <a href="/wiki/Vicarage_Road" title="Vicarage Road">Vicarage Road</a> after clashing heads with an opponent. He was taken to the hospital for tests and was in recovering condition.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> It was later determined his <a href="/wiki/Nasal_septum_perforation" title="Nasal septum perforation">nasal septum ruptured</a>, which looked like a major injury, but turned out to be only minor.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> On 8 November 2015, Immobile scored his first goal for Sevilla in the 36th minute as they emerged victorious in a 32 <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_La_Liga" title="201516 La Liga">La Liga</a> home win over <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> In November, the obligation to buy clause was exercised when Immobile made his fifth appearance, buying him outright for 11 million plus the 3 million for the loan spell.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Loan_to_Torino">Loan to Torino</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Loan to Torino">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 14 January 2016, Immobile returned to Torino on loan until the end of <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Serie_A" title="201516 Serie A">201516 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Two days later on his return debut, he scored the opening goal of a 42 home victory over <a href="/wiki/Frosinone_Calcio" title="Frosinone Calcio">Frosinone</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On 14 February, he scored a brace, in a 31 win away against <a href="/wiki/U.S._Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Città di Palermo">Palermo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> On 22 March, it was determined he sustained a muscular injury at the half time mark in a <a href="/wiki/Derby_della_Mole" title="Derby della Mole">derby</a> with Juventus two days prior, and would be sidelined for a month.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lazio">Lazio</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Lazio">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 27 July 2016, Immobile signed with <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a> for a fee of 8.75 million (plus 700,000 commission to agents).<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> On 21 August, Immobile scored on his debut in Lazio's opening match of a 43 away win over <a href="/wiki/Atalanta_B.C." title="Atalanta B.C.">Atalanta</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Immobile finished the season with 23 league goals in 36 appearances plus 3 goals in the Coppa Italia,<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> surpassing his total when he won the <i><a href="/wiki/Capocannoniere" title="Capocannoniere">Capocannoniere</a></i> with Torino in the 201314 season, though this time he did not win the <i>Capocannoniere</i>, losing it to Bosnian striker <a href="/wiki/Edin_D%C5%BEeko" title="Edin Deko">Edin Deko</a> of cross-town rivals <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a>, who scored 29 league goals.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 August 2017, Immobile scored the opening two goals of the <a href="/wiki/2017_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2017 Supercoppa Italiana">Supercoppa Italiana</a>; Lazio won with a final score of 32 over Juventus.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> On 10 September, in Lazio's third match of the season, he scored a hat-trick and got an assist in a 41 home win over <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> On 21 October, Immobile extended with Lazio until 2022.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> On 6 January 2018, Immobile scored four goals in the first half away to <a href="/wiki/S.P.A.L._2013" class="mw-redirect" title="S.P.A.L. 2013">SPAL</a>, the first Lazio player to score multiple hat-tricks in a season in 16 years; Lazio eventually won the match 52.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On 22 February 2018, Immobile scored a hat-trick in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Europa_League" title="201718 UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a> round of 32 second leg home to <a href="/wiki/FC_Steaua_Bucure%C8%99ti" class="mw-redirect" title="FC Steaua Bucureti">Steaua Bucureti</a> in a 51 win, which allowed Lazio to qualify, 52 on aggregate, to the round of 16.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> On 31 March 2018, Immobile scored twice in Lazio's 62 home win over <a href="/wiki/Benevento_Calcio" title="Benevento Calcio">Benevento</a>, his 36th goal of the season, breaking <a href="/wiki/Giorgio_Chinaglia" title="Giorgio Chinaglia">Giorgio Chinaglia</a>'s previous record for most goals scored by a Lazio player in a single season, by two goals.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Immobile ended the season with 29 goals in 33 appearances, winning the <i>Capocannoniere</i> jointly with Inter's <a href="/wiki/Mauro_Icardi" title="Mauro Icardi">Mauro Icardi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-laziocap_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-laziocap-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 3 November 2019, he scored his 100th goal for Lazio in a 21 away win over Milan.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> On 26 July 2020, Immobile scored a hat-trick in a 51 win against Hellas Verona.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> Immobile finished the season with 36 goals, winning the <i>Capocannoniere</i> and equaling <a href="/wiki/Gino_Rossetti" title="Gino Rossetti">Gino Rossetti</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_Higua%C3%ADn" title="Gonzalo Higuaín">Gonzalo Higuaín</a>'s all-time <a href="/wiki/Football_records_and_statistics_in_Italy#Most_goals_in_a_single_Serie_A_season" title="Football records and statistics in Italy">record for most goals in a Serie A season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-cap_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cap-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> He also won the <a href="/wiki/European_Golden_Shoe" title="European Golden Shoe">European Golden Shoe</a> for the first time in his career, becoming the first Italian player or player from Serie A to win the award since <a href="/wiki/Francesco_Totti" title="Francesco Totti">Francesco Totti</a> in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-cap_69-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cap-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Moreover, he set a new <a href="/wiki/Football_records_and_statistics_in_Italy#Most_penalty_kicks_scored_in_a_single_Serie_A_season" title="Football records and statistics in Italy">record for most penalties scored in a single Serie A season</a>, with 14.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 31 August 2020, Immobile signed a five-year contract extension with Lazio.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> On 20 October 2020, he scored a goal in a 31 win over his former club Borussia Dortmund in the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League" title="202021 UEFA Champions League">202021 UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:20150616_-_Portugal_-_Italie_-_Gen%C3%A8ve_-_Ciro_Immobile_au_milieu_de_la_d%C3%A9fense_portugaise.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/20150616_-_Portugal_-_Italie_-_Gen%C3%A8ve_-_Ciro_Immobile_au_milieu_de_la_d%C3%A9fense_portugaise.jpg/220px-20150616_-_Portugal_-_Italie_-_Gen%C3%A8ve_-_Ciro_Immobile_au_milieu_de_la_d%C3%A9fense_portugaise.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/20150616_-_Portugal_-_Italie_-_Gen%C3%A8ve_-_Ciro_Immobile_au_milieu_de_la_d%C3%A9fense_portugaise.jpg/330px-20150616_-_Portugal_-_Italie_-_Gen%C3%A8ve_-_Ciro_Immobile_au_milieu_de_la_d%C3%A9fense_portugaise.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/20150616_-_Portugal_-_Italie_-_Gen%C3%A8ve_-_Ciro_Immobile_au_milieu_de_la_d%C3%A9fense_portugaise.jpg/440px-20150616_-_Portugal_-_Italie_-_Gen%C3%A8ve_-_Ciro_Immobile_au_milieu_de_la_d%C3%A9fense_portugaise.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4638" data-file-height="3092" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:20150616_-_Portugal_-_Italie_-_Gen%C3%A8ve_-_Ciro_Immobile_au_milieu_de_la_d%C3%A9fense_portugaise.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Immobile taking on the Portuguese defence in a June 2015 friendly in <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a>, Switzerland</div></div></div>
<p>On 2 March 2014, he received his first call-up to the senior national team by <a href="/wiki/Cesare_Prandelli" title="Cesare Prandelli">Cesare Prandelli</a>, for a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a> three days later.<sup id="cite_ref-first_cap_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-first_cap-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut as a substitute for <a href="/wiki/Alessio_Cerci" title="Alessio Cerci">Alessio Cerci</a> after 69 minutes as Spain eventually won 10.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 May 2014, Immobile was named in Italy's provisional 30-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> and on 1 June he was named in the final 23-man squad.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> On 8 June, he scored a hat-trick in Italy's final World Cup warm-up match, a 53 unofficial win over Brazilian club side <a href="/wiki/Fluminense_FC" title="Fluminense FC">Fluminense</a>. Immobile made his competitive debut in Italy's opening 21 win over <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> in <a href="/wiki/Manaus" title="Manaus">Manaus</a> on 14 June, playing the last 17 minutes in place of <a href="/wiki/Mario_Balotelli" title="Mario Balotelli">Mario Balotelli</a> who scored the Italian winner.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first official international goal in the third minute of a 20 friendly victory against the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a> on 4 September 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 31 May 2016, Immobile was named to <a href="/wiki/Antonio_Conte" title="Antonio Conte">Antonio Conte</a>'s 23-man Italy squad for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Although primarily a main striker, Immobile is capable of playing anywhere along the front-line. A quick <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a>, Immobile is primarily known for his offensive movement off the ball, as well as his ability to make attacking runs and exploit spaces.<sup id="cite_ref-Ciro_Immobile_is_primed_and_ready_to_be_Italy&#39;s_new_Toto_Schillaci_80-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ciro_Immobile_is_primed_and_ready_to_be_Italy&#39;s_new_Toto_Schillaci-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> His main characteristics are his eye for goal and finishing ability with either foot, as well as his physical attributes; he also possesses solid technique, and is effective in the air.<sup id="cite_ref-Ciro_Immobile_is_primed_and_ready_to_be_Italy&#39;s_new_Toto_Schillaci_80-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ciro_Immobile_is_primed_and_ready_to_be_Italy&#39;s_new_Toto_Schillaci-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> In addition to his offensive capabilities and goalscoring ability, he is also a hard-working player, known for his willingness to chase down the ball and press opponents when not in possession;<sup id="cite_ref-Ciro_Immobile_is_primed_and_ready_to_be_Italy&#39;s_new_Toto_Schillaci_80-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ciro_Immobile_is_primed_and_ready_to_be_Italy&#39;s_new_Toto_Schillaci-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> he also possesses good link-up play,<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> which enables him to provide assists for teammates, in addition to scoring goals himself.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> He is also an accurate <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty</a> taker.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> A prolific goalscorer, he is considered by pundits to be one of the best strikers in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_2">Club</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ciro_Immobile&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Club">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
